 ve keval ek mukaable main haare hai

 yahaan varanasi ke mashhoor shmashaan manikarnika ghat kii baat ho rahi he

 bataaya jaataa he ki yahaan kai saalon se yah parampara chali aa rahi he
 Faced with the cluttered eyes of the society, the citizens, with a desire to earn merit, have faithfully kept the tradition going on for centuries, like this every year
 manikarnika ke shmashaan ghat main bane mashaan baba mandir main sadhana ke liye varanasi ke alaava chandauli, mirzapur or mumbai samet kai shaharon se nagarvadhuen ai thim
 He first decorated the crematorium Nath Baba in the temple
 iske baad wo jalati chitaaon ke paas saje manch main puri raat thirakati raheen

 tab aisi parampara tha ki jab bhi mandir banwaaya jaataa tha, uske baad vahaan bhajan-kirthan kaa aayojan hota tha

 raja kii ore se nagarvadhuon ko nimantran bheja gaya

 ve puri raat baba ke darbar main nrity karti raheen or mannate maangati raheen ki unhen agle janm main behatar jindagi mili or roji-roti ke liye apane tan kaa sauda naa karnaa pade
 In 2014-15, a total of 292 people lost their lives in railway accidents
 is baat kii jaankaree rajyasabha menrel mantrisuresh prabhu ne ek sawaal ke likhit jawaab main di
 He told the Rajya Sabha in response to a question that a total of 135 major accidents took place in 2014-15, out of which 50 were at unmanned gates and six accidents at watchman gates
 150 se bhi zyada logon ne ganvaai jaanaprabhu ne bataaya ki 2014-15 main rail phatakon par huyi durghatnaon main 161 logon kii maut hui thi
 He said that till November 11 this year, there were 69 accidents in which 92 people died
 rail mantri ke mutabikphatakonper durghatanon ko rokane ke liye kai upaay kiye gaye hai
 These measures include the introduction of an SMS campaign for social awareness
 bachche ko berth dene ke liye lenaa hoga puraa tikmogar aap apane 12 saal tak ke bachche ko lekar rail main yatra karte hai to aapako uskaa ab puraa tikat khareednaa hoga
 Actually, the railways have decided not to give berths if children take half tickets
 railway niyamon ke mutabik 5 saal se lekar 12 saal tak bacchon kaa aadha tikat lagata he
 At present, these children get full berths despite the half-ticket for booking tickets in reserved category
 lekin railway ne agle saal 10 april se is niyam main badlaav kar diya he
 From 10 April 2016, half of the children of 5 years to 12 years will not get a berth on taking tickets
 agar aapako bachche ke liye berth chahie to aapako puraa tikat khareednaa padegaa

 pakistani sainikon kii ghuspaith or do bhartiya sainikon kii berahami se hatya ke maamle main bharat ne pakistan ke saamne kadaa virodh darj karaayaa he

 videsh sachiv ranjan mathai ne pakistani ucchayukta salmaan bashir se kaha ki pakistan sarkaar tatkaal is ghatana kii jaanch karaae, jo har pahalu se antarrashtriya niyamon ke khilaaf he
 The Foreign Secretary reminded the Pakistan High Commissioner of the meeting between the two countries on December 27, in which there was talk of increasing mutual trust and honest adherence to the Line of Control
 haalanki is maamle par salmaan bashir ne kuch bhi kehane se inkaar kar diya

 pradhanmantri ne videsh mantralay, enese or sena pramukh se golibari par puri report maangi he
